
-----------
QUERY:
--
-- GEOMETRY
--

-- Back off displayed precision a little bit to reduce platform-to-platform
-- variation in results.
SET extra_float_digits TO -3;
RESULT:
	[]

-----------
QUERY:


--
-- Points
--

SELECT center(f1) AS center
   FROM BOX_TBL;
RESULT:
	[('(1,1)',), ('(2,2)',), ('(-5,-4)',), ('(2.5,3)',), ('(3,3)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT (@@ f1) AS center
   FROM BOX_TBL;
RESULT:
	[('(1,1)',), ('(2,2)',), ('(-5,-4)',), ('(2.5,3)',), ('(3,3)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT point(f1) AS center
   FROM CIRCLE_TBL;
RESULT:
	[('(5,1)',), ('(1,2)',), ('(1,3)',), ('(1,2)',), ('(100,200)',), ('(100,1)',), ('(3,5)',), ('(3,5)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT (@@ f1) AS center
   FROM CIRCLE_TBL;
RESULT:
	[('(5,1)',), ('(1,2)',), ('(1,3)',), ('(1,2)',), ('(100,200)',), ('(100,1)',), ('(3,5)',), ('(3,5)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT (@@ f1) AS center
   FROM POLYGON_TBL
   WHERE (# f1) > 2;
RESULT:
	[('(1.33333333333,1.33333333333)',), ('(2.33333333333,1.33333333333)',), ('(4,5)',), ('(4,5)',), ('(4,3)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


-- /* REPLACED */ ''is horizontal/* REPLACED */ '' function
SELECT p1.f1
   FROM POINT_TBL p1
   WHERE ishorizontal(p1.f1, point '(0,0)');
RESULT:
	[('(0,0)',), ('(-10,0)',), ('(1e-300,-1e-300)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


-- /* REPLACED */ ''is horizontal/* REPLACED */ '' operator
SELECT p1.f1
   FROM POINT_TBL p1
   WHERE p1.f1 ?- point '(0,0)';
RESULT:
	[('(0,0)',), ('(-10,0)',), ('(1e-300,-1e-300)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


-- /* REPLACED */ ''is vertical/* REPLACED */ '' function
SELECT p1.f1
   FROM POINT_TBL p1
   WHERE isvertical(p1.f1, point '(5.1,34.5)');
RESULT:
	[('(5.1,34.5)',)]

-----------
QUERY:


-- /* REPLACED */ ''is vertical/* REPLACED */ '' operator
SELECT p1.f1
   FROM POINT_TBL p1
   WHERE p1.f1 ?| point '(5.1,34.5)';
RESULT:
	[('(5.1,34.5)',)]

QUERY:


--
-- Lines
--

-- Vertical
SELECT s FROM LINE_TBL WHERE ?| s;
RESULT:
	[('{1,0,5}',), ('{-1,0,3}',)]

QUERY:


-- Horizontal
SELECT s FROM LINE_TBL WHERE ?- s;
RESULT:
	[('{0,-1,5}',), ('{0,3,0}',), ('{0,-1,3}',)]

-- Check index behavior for circles

CREATE INDEX gcircleind ON circle_tbl USING gist (f1);
RESULT:
	[]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT * FROM circle_tbl WHERE f1 && circle(point(1,-2), 1)
    ORDER BY area(f1);
RESULT:
	[('<(1,2),3>',), ('<(1,3),5>',), ('<(1,2),100>',), ('<(100,1),115>',)]

-----------
QUERY:


EXPLAIN (COSTS OFF)
SELECT * FROM circle_tbl WHERE f1 && circle(point(1,-2), 1)
    ORDER BY area(f1);
RESULT:
	[('Sort',), ('  Sort Key: (area(f1))',), ('  ->  Seq Scan on circle_tbl',), ("        Filter: (f1 && '<(1,-2),1>'::circle)",)]

-----------
QUERY:

SELECT * FROM circle_tbl WHERE f1 && circle(point(1,-2), 1)
    ORDER BY area(f1);
RESULT:
	[('<(1,2),3>',), ('<(1,3),5>',), ('<(1,2),100>',), ('<(100,1),115>',)]

-----------
QUERY:


-- Check index behavior for polygons

CREATE INDEX gpolygonind ON polygon_tbl USING gist (f1);
RESULT:
	[]

-----------
QUERY:


SELECT * FROM polygon_tbl WHERE f1 @> '((1,1),(2,2),(2,1))'::polygon
    ORDER BY (poly_center(f1))[0];
RESULT:
	[('((2,0),(2,4),(0,0))',)]

-----------
QUERY:


EXPLAIN (COSTS OFF)
SELECT * FROM polygon_tbl WHERE f1 @> '((1,1),(2,2),(2,1))'::polygon
    ORDER BY (poly_center(f1))[0];
RESULT:
	[('Sort',), ('  Sort Key: ((poly_center(f1))[0])',), ('  ->  Seq Scan on polygon_tbl',), ("        Filter: (f1 @> '((1,1),(2,2),(2,1))'::polygon)",)]

-----------
QUERY:

SELECT * FROM polygon_tbl WHERE f1 @> '((1,1),(2,2),(2,1))'::polygon
    ORDER BY (poly_center(f1))[0];
RESULT:
	[('((2,0),(2,4),(0,0))',)]

QUERY:


-- test non-error-throwing API for some core types
SELECT pg_input_is_valid('(1', 'circle');
RESULT:
	[(False,)]

-----------
QUERY:

SELECT * FROM pg_input_error_info('1,', 'circle');
RESULT:
	[('invalid input syntax for type circle: "1,"', None, None, '22P02')]

-----------
QUERY:

SELECT pg_input_is_valid('(1,2),-1', 'circle');
RESULT:
	[(False,)]

-----------
QUERY:

SELECT * FROM pg_input_error_info('(1,2),-1', 'circle');
RESULT:
	[('invalid input syntax for type circle: "(1,2),-1"', None, None, '22P02')]
